<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жир.html>жир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жировой.html>жирово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žirovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fat; fatty, adipose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жировой.html>жирова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ткань.html>ткань</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žirovája</b> tkanʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fatty/adipose</b> tissue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жировой.html>жирова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žirovája</b> klétka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fat</b> cell</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жировой.html>жирово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перерождение.html>перерожде́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žirovóje</b> pereroždénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fatty</b> degeneration</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жировой.html>жирово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žirovóje</b> jajcó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wind egg</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жировой.html>жирова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:промышленность.html>промы́шленность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žirovája</b> promýšlennostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fat</b> products industry</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жирок.html>жиро́к</a> (25455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жир.html>жир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жирок.html>жиро́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žirók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жирок.html>жи́рка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жирок.html>жи́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жирок.html>жи́рков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жир.html>жир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small fat deposit in a tissue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reserve, stock, surplus</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жительница.html>жи́тельница</a> (25033)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:житель.html>жи́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:житие.html>житие</a> (25530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">житиѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žitьje</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to live</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:житье.html>житьё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.

***жито.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жито.html>жи́то</a> (30658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žito</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grain, corn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*geit-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*GʷeHi-to-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жито.html>жи́то</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žíto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жито.html>жи́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жито.html>жи́та</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жито.html>жи́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grain (any unground grain, such as rye, wheat, buckwheat, millet, barley, maize, oats)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rye</li></ol>

***жить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a> (118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žiti</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">жыць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žycʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">жи́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žýty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷeih₃w-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to live</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">gyventi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">जीवति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jīvati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīvō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прожить.html>прожи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to live
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>žitʹ</b> na širókuju nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to live in a grand style</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reside</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Note the stress in the past negative:

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>

***житься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>жи́ться</a> (8734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>жи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>живётся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неплохо.html>непло́хо</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>živjótsja</b> neplóxo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is quite well off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>живётся</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak vam <b>živjótsja</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how's life?; how is life treating you?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>жило́сь</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>жи́лось</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak vam tam <b>žilósʹ/žílosʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how did you get on there?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:житься.html>живётся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú ne <b>živjótsja</b> na odnóm méste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is never content to stay in one place</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жмуриться.html>жму́риться</a> (14482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">жму́рить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žmúritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жмуриться.html>жму́риться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žmúritʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажмуриться.html>зажму́риться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to screw up one's eye(s), to narrow one's eyes, to blink (e.g. under the bright sunlight)</li>
<li>to shut one's eyes tightly (especially in the perfective form)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">жму́рить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žmúritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***жопа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́па</a> (6519)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain, presumed to derive from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> form which cannot be easily reconstructed. According to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Vasmer" class="extiw" title="w:Max Vasmer">Vasmer</a>, two probable hypotheses are:
</p>
<ul><li>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gap</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rubbernecker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gapić się</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жупа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">župa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">жу́па</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žúpa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">salt mine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́па</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žópa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́пы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жоп</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">жо́пный</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">жо́пка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ass, arse (<i>the buttocks of a person or animal</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуть.html>подви́нь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́пу</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Podvínʹ <b>žópu</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Move your <b>ass</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> middle of nowhere, Bumfuck
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> како́й-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́пе</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó dom v kakój-to <b>žópe</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">His house is someplace <b>in the middle of nowhere</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a difficult situation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глубокий.html>глубо́кую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́пу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ v glubókuju <b>žópu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be in deep <b>shit</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"> — <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>таку́ю</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́пу</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́л</a>! </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="в качестве сказуемого">предик.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a> </span><span style="display: none"></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"> — <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>Дело</a> — <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́па</a></span>! </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>Каки́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́гут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открыться.html>откры́ться</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>По́лная</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:жопа.html>жо́па</a></span>! <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> больше <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a>! </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

***жрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жрать.html>жрать</a> (3516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жьрати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žĭrati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьrati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷerh₃-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to devour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">devour</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">voracity</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жрать.html>жрать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žratʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожрать.html>пожра́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сожрать.html>сожра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of an animal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gobble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guzzle <i>(alcohol)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guzzle <i>(fuel or power)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of an insect</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sting, to bite</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жребий.html>жре́бий</a> (13991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жрѣбии</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žrěbii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žerbьjь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">же́ребей</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žérebej</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жребий.html>жре́бий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žrébij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жребий.html>жре́бия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жребий.html>жре́бии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жребий.html>жре́биев</a></b>)

<li>fate, destiny</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жрец.html>жрец</a> (11135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьrьcь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žьrti</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьcь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*girʔ-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*GʷrH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***жужжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жужжать.html>жужжа́ть</a> (11549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жужжать.html>жужжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žužžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зажужжать.html>зажужжа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прожужжать.html>прожужжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hum, to buzz, to drone, to whirr</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say something</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fatigue someone by saying too much or by repetition of the same thing (<a href = vnd.unilang:прожужжать.html>прожужжа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a> прожужжал)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žukъ</i>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">жу́льнич(ать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žúlʹnič(atʹ)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cheat, to swindle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жульничество.html>жу́льничество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žúlʹničestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жульничество.html>жу́льничества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жульничество.html>жу́льничества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жульничество.html>жу́льничеств</a></b>)
</p>

***журавль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:журавль.html>жура́вль</a> (12469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Middle Ukrainian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">журавлин</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuravlyn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">журавлинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuravlyn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:журавлиный.html>журавли́ное</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuravlynoe</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">журавовъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuravov</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жеравие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeravie</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жеравець</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeravecĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жеравлины</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeravliny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жералины</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeraliny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жеравлиныя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeravlinyja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">жералиныя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeralinyja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žeravjь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gerh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to call hoarsely</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*žeravъ</i> is also interpreted as the fusion of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ger-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gera-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*awis</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂éwis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gerh₂-</i>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">журавель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuravjelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">жораў</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žóraŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">жерав</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žerav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">жеравль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žeravlĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Czech <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">jeřáb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_the_Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:History of the Czech language">Old Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-ocs">žeřáv</i>, Macedonian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">жерав</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žerav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old East Slavic журавь, жеравль, Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">żuraw</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">ždral</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ждра̑л</i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ждрӓо</i>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">жѐра̄в</i>, Slovak <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">žeriav</i>, Slovene <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">žerjàv</i>, Upper Sorbian žoraw, Lower Sorbian žorawa, Ukrainian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">журавель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žuravelʹ</span><span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журавль.html>жура́вль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">žurávlʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журавль.html>журавля́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журавль.html>журавли́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журавль.html>журавле́й</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:журавлиный.html>журавли́ный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crane <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bird</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
